<tr class="hlist noprint" style="background-color: #eee;">
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<ul>
<li>← <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2011_French_Open_(tennis)" title="2011 French Open (tennis)">2011</a></li>
<li><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/French_Open_(tennis)" title="French Open (tennis)">French Open</a></b></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2013_French_Open" title="2013 French Open">2013</a> →</li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>The <b>2012 French Open</b> (also known as <b>Roland Garros</b>, after the famous French aviator) was a tennis tournament played on outdoor clay courts. It was the 111th edition of the <a href="/wiki/French_Open" title="French Open">French Open</a>, and took place at the Stade Roland Garros from 27 May until 11 June 2012.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Rafael_Nadal" title="Rafael Nadal">Rafael Nadal</a> won the tournament for the third year in succession, and the seventh time in eight years, defeating first-time Roland Garros finalist <a href="/wiki/Novak_Djokovic" title="Novak Djokovic">Novak Djokovic</a>. His seventh title broke <a href="/wiki/Bj%C3%B6rn_Borg" title="Björn Borg">Björn Borg</a>'s record of six French Open Men's Singles titles, and equalled <a href="/wiki/Chris_Evert" title="Chris Evert">Chris Evert</a>'s record for most French Open titles won by a man or woman. <a href="/wiki/Li_Na" title="Li Na">Li Na</a> was unsuccessful in her title defence, being defeated in the fourth round by <a href="/wiki/Yaroslava_Shvedova" title="Yaroslava Shvedova">Yaroslava Shvedova</a>. <a href="/wiki/Maria_Sharapova" title="Maria Sharapova">Maria Sharapova</a> defeated 21st seed <a href="/wiki/Sara_Errani" title="Sara Errani">Sara Errani</a> in the final to win her first French Open title, to complete a career Grand Slam, and to return to the World No. 1 ranking for the first time in four years.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup></p>
<p>This championship was the second time in grand slam history that two <a href="/wiki/Grand_Slam_(tennis)#Multiple_Career_Grand_Slams" title="Grand Slam (tennis)">multiple slam sets</a> were accomplished in two different disciplines, and that was <a href="/wiki/Mahesh_Bhupathi" title="Mahesh Bhupathi">Mahesh Bhupathi</a> won his first multiple slam in Mixed Doubles, and <a href="/wiki/Esther_Vergeer" title="Esther Vergeer">Esther Vergeer</a> won her second multiple slam set in Women's Wheelchair Doubles. At the <a href="/wiki/1969_US_Open_(tennis)" title="1969 US Open (tennis)">1969 US Open</a>, Rod Laver won his first multiple slam set in Men's Singles, and his fellow countryman <a href="/wiki/Ken_Rosewall" title="Ken Rosewall">Ken Rosewall</a> did in Men's Doubles for the first time. This would occur again for the third time at the <a href="/wiki/2013_French_Open" title="2013 French Open">2013 French Open</a>.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Tournament">Tournament</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_French_Open&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Tournament">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:RolandGarrosCentral.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1553" data-file-width="2309" height="148" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/RolandGarrosCentral.jpg/220px-RolandGarrosCentral.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/RolandGarrosCentral.jpg/330px-RolandGarrosCentral.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/RolandGarrosCentral.jpg/440px-RolandGarrosCentral.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:RolandGarrosCentral.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Court Philippe Chatrier where the Finals of the French Open take place.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The 2012 French Open was the one hundred and eleventh edition of the French Open and was held at <a href="/wiki/Stade_Roland_Garros" title="Stade Roland Garros">Stade Roland Garros</a> in Paris.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> The Men's Singles Final was won by Rafael Nadal by defeating Novak Djokovic in the final. By winning his seventh title at Roland Garros, Nadal surpassed Borg's overall titles record to become the most successful tennis player in French Open history. The tournament was an event run by the <a href="/wiki/International_Tennis_Federation" title="International Tennis Federation">International Tennis Federation</a> (ITF) and is part of the <a href="/wiki/2012_ATP_World_Tour" title="2012 ATP World Tour">2012 ATP World Tour</a> and the <a href="/wiki/2012_WTA_Tour" title="2012 WTA Tour">2012 WTA Tour</a> calendars under the Grand Slam category. The tournament consisted of both men's and women's singles and doubles draws as well as a mixed doubles event.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup></p>
<p>There was a singles and doubles events for both boys and girls (players under 18), which is part of the Grade A category of tournaments, and singles and doubles events for men's and women's <a href="/wiki/Wheelchair_tennis" title="Wheelchair tennis">wheelchair tennis</a> players as part of the NEC tour under the Grand Slam category. The tournament was played on clay courts and took place over a series of twenty courts, including the three main showcourts, <a href="/wiki/Stade_Roland_Garros#Court_Philippe_Chatrier" title="Stade Roland Garros">Court Philippe Chatrier</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Court_Suzanne_Lenglen" title="Court Suzanne Lenglen">Court Suzanne Lenglen</a> and <a href="/wiki/Stade_Roland_Garros#Court_1" title="Stade Roland Garros">Court 1</a>.</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Prize_money_and_ranking_points">Prize money and ranking points</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_French_Open&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Prize money and ranking points">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>For 2012, the prize money purse was increased to €18,718,000 from €17,520,000 in 2011. The prize money and points breakdown is as follows:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Day_5_.2831_May.29">Day 5 (31 May)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_French_Open&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Day 5 (31 May)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.rolandgarros.com/en_FR/scores/schedule/schedule10.html" rel="nofollow">Schedule of Play</a></li>
<li>Seeds out:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2012_French_Open_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_Singles" title="2012 French Open – Men's Singles">Men's Singles</a>: <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Day_6_.281_June.29">Day 6 (1 June)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_French_Open&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Day 6 (1 June)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.rolandgarros.com/en_FR/scores/schedule/schedule11.html" rel="nofollow">Schedule of Play</a></li>
<li>Seeds out:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2012_French_Open_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_Singles" title="2012 French Open – Men's Singles">Men's Singles</a>: <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/France" title="France"><img alt="France" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Gilles_Simon" title="Gilles Simon">Gilles Simon</a> [11], <span <p><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain"><img alt="Spain" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="750" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/9a/Flag_of_Spain.svg/23px-Flag_of_Spain.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/9a/Flag_of_Spain.svg/35px-Flag_of_Spain.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/9a/Flag_of_Spain.svg/45px-Flag_of_Spain.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <b><a href="/wiki/Rafael_Nadal" title="Rafael Nadal">Rafael Nadal</a></b> defeated <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia"><img alt="Serbia" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="900" data-file-width="1350" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/ff/Flag_of_Serbia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Serbia.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/ff/Flag_of_Serbia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Serbia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/ff/Flag_of_Serbia.svg/45px-Flag_of_Serbia.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Novak_Djokovic" title="Novak Djokovic">Novak Djokovic</a> 6–4, 6–3, 2–6, 7–5</p>
<dl>
<dd><small>*It was Nadal's eleventh career Grand Slam title and his 7th title at French Open. It was his 4th title of the year, 50th title overall.</small></dd>
</dl>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Singles_seeds">Singles seeds</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2012_French_Open&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Singles seeds">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
